
Predict expression modulation targets
=====================================

Cameo provides algorithms to search for genes or reactions that can be
over or down regulated in order to achieve a given biological objective.

.. code:: ipython3

    from cameo import models



.. raw:: html

    





.. raw:: html

    




Load the E. coli core model.

.. code:: ipython3

    model = models.bigg.e_coli_core

Flux Scanning based on Enforced Objective Flux
----------------------------------------------

.. code:: ipython3

    from cameo.strain_design.deterministic.flux_variability_based import FSEOF

.. code:: ipython3

    fseof = FSEOF(model)

.. code:: ipython3

    fseof.run(target=model.reactions.EX_succ_e)




.. raw:: html

    
    <strong>Model:</strong> e_coli_core</br>
    <strong>Enforced objective:</strong> EX_succ_e</br>
    <strong>Primary objective:</strong> Maximize
    -1.0*BIOMASS_Ecoli_core_w_GAM_reverse_712e5 + 1.0*BIOMASS_Ecoli_core_w_GAM</br>
    <br>

Differential flux variability analysis
--------------------------------------

Compares flux ranges of a reference model to a set of models that have
been parameterized to lie on a grid of evenly spaced points in the
n-dimensional production envelope (n being the number of reaction bounds
to be varied).

.. code:: ipython3

    from cameo.flux_analysis.analysis import phenotypic_phase_plane
    from cameo.strain_design.deterministic import DifferentialFVA

Succinate production
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

The production envelope looks like this.

.. code:: ipython3

    production_envelope = phenotypic_phase_plane(model, 
                                                 variables=[model.reactions.BIOMASS_Ecoli_core_w_GAM],
                                                 objective=model.metabolites.succ_e)
    production_envelope.plot(height=400)

Set up a model that represents a reference state (in this case a model
with a constrained growth rate).

.. code:: ipython3

    model.reactions.EX_o2_e.lower_bound = 0
    reference_model = model.copy()
    biomass_rxn = reference_model.reactions.BIOMASS_Ecoli_core_w_GAM
    biomass_rxn.lower_bound = 0.
    target = reference_model.metabolites.succ_e

Set up the differential flux variability analysis strain design method.

.. code:: ipython3

    diffFVA = DifferentialFVA(design_space_model=model,
                              reference_model=reference_model,
                              objective=target,
                              variables=[biomass_rxn],
                              normalize_ranges_by=biomass_rxn,
                              points=10)

Run differential flux variability analysis (only on the surface of the
production envelope)

.. code:: ipython3

    result = diffFVA.run(surface_only=True)




.. code:: ipython3

    result.solutions

          return new Date();

          window._bokeh_onload_callbacks.forEach(function(callback) { callback() });
          delete window._bokeh_onload_callbacks
          console.info("Bokeh: all callbacks have finished");
        }
      
        function load_libs(js_urls, callback) {
          window._bokeh_onload_callbacks.push(callback);
          if (window._bokeh_is_loading > 0) {
            console.log("Bokeh: BokehJS is being loaded, scheduling callback at", now());
            return null;
          }
          if (js_urls == null || js_urls.length === 0) {
            run_callbacks();
            return null;
          }
          console.log("Bokeh: BokehJS not loaded, scheduling load and callback at", now());
          window._bokeh_is_loading = js_urls.length;
          for (var i = 0; i < js_urls.length; i++) {
            var url = js_urls[i];
            var s = document.createElement('script');
            s.src = url;
            s.async = false;
            s.onreadystatechange = s.onload = function() {
              window._bokeh_is_loading--;
              if (window._bokeh_is_loading === 0) {
                console.log("Bokeh: all BokehJS libraries loaded");
                run_callbacks()
              }
            };
            s.onerror = function() {
              console.warn("failed to load library " + url);
            };
            console.log("Bokeh: injecting script tag for BokehJS library: ", url);
            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(s);
          }

      <script>
       /* Closure to make sure data only applies to this map. */
       (function() {
           /* data from python */
           var data = get_data();
    
           function load_lib(url, callback) {
               /** Dynamically load a JavaScript file */
               var s = document.createElement('script');
               s.src = url;
               s.async = true;
               s.onreadystatechange = s.onload = callback;
               s.onerror = function() {
                   console.warn('Failed to load library ' + url);
               };
               document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(s);
           }
    
           function check_global_and_load(name, url, callback) {
               /** Look for the name in the global scope. If it isn't present, then
                  load the library at url. Returns the object. */
               if (window[name] !== undefined) {
                   callback(window[name]);
               } else {
                   load_lib(url, function() {
                       callback(window[name]);
                   });
               }
           }
    
           function draw_escher(escher) {
               /** Get data and draw */
               var load = function(t_map_data, t_model_data, t_options) {
                   escher.Builder(t_map_data, t_model_data, data.builder_embed_css,
                                  escher.libs.d3_select('#' + data.id), t_options);
               }
    
               // for the static site, use the url attributes for the map and model
               // information
               if (data.static_site_index !== null) {
                   escher.static.load_map_model_from_url(data.map_download_url, data.model_download_url,
                                                         data.static_site_index, data.options, load);
               } else {
                   load(data.map_data, data.model_data, data.options);
               }
           }
    
           // Load dependencies and draw
           if (typeof define === 'function' && define.amd) {
               // require.js is available: use it to load escher
               require.config({
                 paths: {
                   escher: '//unpkg.com/escher-vis@1.6.0/js/dist/escher.min',
                 },
                 // Override urlArgs that adds ?v= to the end of the escher URL and
                 // messes up unpkg links. Honestly, I'm not sure if this will lead
                 // to downstream bugs in the notebook, but they really shouldn't be
                 // doing this cache-busting anyway.
                 urlArgs: null,
               })
               require([ 'escher' ], function(escher) {
                   draw_escher(escher);
               })
           } else {
               // require.js not available: dynamically load escher
               check_global_and_load('escher', '//unpkg.com/escher-vis@1.6.0/js/dist/escher.min.js', function(escher) {
                   draw_escher(escher);
               })
           }
